# claude-mgr вҖ” project context for Claude Code sessions

A **read-mostly governance CLI** for the user's large Claude Code harness (inventory / conflicts / `config show-effective` / doctor / snapshot-rollback / remove-update). Zero-runtime-dependency Node ESM, Windows-hardened, **dry-run-by-default**, lives OUTSIDE Claude Code's loader. The user is a non-coder ("vibe coding") вҖ” reply in Chinese.

cosmetic)гҖӮ**жҲ‘зҡ„ trust-but-verify жҠ“дәҶ IDE еҒҮиӯҰжҠҘ + дёҖдёӘзңҹй—®йўҳеҒҮиұЎ:**(1)ж–°иҜҠж–ӯжҠҘ `main.go:663 undefined: healthItems` + throwaway ж®Ӣз•ҷвҖ”вҖ”дәІйӘҢ `go build` йҖҖ 0гҖҒhealthItems зҡ„"й—ӘеұҸвҶ’жёІжҹ“й”Ғ uiLangвҶ’жҮ’еҸ–ж•°"зҺҜиҠӮ;line 767 иҜӯиЁҖеҲҮжҚўеңЁ showSplash еқ—еҶ…=иҝӣд»ӘиЎЁзӣҳеҗҺиҜӯиЁҖеӣәе®ҡ,ж•…зңҹе®һйЎәеәҸдёӢиЎҢж Үйўҳз”ЁдјҡиҜқиҜӯиЁҖеҶ»з»“жӯЈзЎ®);дҝ®жӯЈйЎәеәҸйҮҚжёІжҹ“ вҶ’ ZH жЎҶжһ¶е®ҢзҫҺ(`[x] agent:broken-agent В· жңӘеҠ иҪҪ` / `дҝ®еӨҚж— ж•Ҳзҡ„ settings.json В· й”ҷиҜҜ` / з©ә-zh и§„еҲҷ `Custom advisory` иӢұж–ҮеӣһйҖҖ / detail `зҠ¶жҖҒ/еҺҹеӣ /ж¶ҲжҒҜ` + Commits `120a307`вҶ’`a108ea7` (categorize/taxonomy/boundary/MCP) pushed. в–· DEFERRED (recorded): output PATH-PRIVACY (absolute paths leak the OS username вҶ’ a `--redact-paths`/relativize option for the future Web-UI export); 2 LOW MCP refinements (`\baws\b` under-matches `awscli`; `sketch`/`screenshot` unanchored вҖ” both dogfood-refine policy, no change). **The original 2026-06-02 user ask вҖ” re-scan P1вҖ“P3 for security/privacy + classify Skill & MCP by purpose вҖ” is now COMPLETE.**

## Per-Unit Definition of Done (every work unit, in order)
1. **Regression** вҖ” full `node --test` green, no regressions.
2. **Code review** вҖ” a SEPARATE `code-reviewer` pass (never self-approve); fix Blocker/High before commit.
3. **Boundary** вҖ” edge cases covered (use the `test/fixtures/` corpus: broken / unicode-paths / long-paths / case-insensitive / вҖҰ).
4. **Acceptance** вҖ” falsifiable criterion (golden-file oracle; "matches golden", never "exit 0").
5. **Git** вҖ” commit on green; **one file = one commit** (data fixtures may commit per-category); push.

## Environment gotchas (verified on this machine)
- Node **v24.14.0**; runner = `node --test` (zero deps). Run from the repo root.
- The **PowerShell tool is unreliable here** вҶ’ use the **Bash tool with POSIX paths** (`/c/Dev/Projects/claude-mgr`).
- Windows **Developer Mode is ON** вҶ’ the dogfood symlink uses `cmd /c mklink /D` (PowerShell `New-Item -SymbolicLink` fails).
- **Subagents may TIME OUT on long tasks here вҖ” but do NOT disable/abandon delegation.** The DoD's SEPARATE `code-reviewer` and `executor` passes MUST stay delegated (never self-author + self-approve вҖ” that gate is the whole point). Mitigate timeouts by scoping each delegated task SMALL (one sub-unit at a time) and **resuming/retrying** a timed-out agent; fall back to a direct Edit ONLY for a tiny fix a reviewer has already prescribed.
- The tool resolves the governed `~/.claude/` and `~/.claude/hooks/lib` via the home dir вҖ” **independent of cwd**, so develop here, not inside `~/.claude/`.
- GitHub remote: `exampleuser-jpg/claude-mgr` (PRIVATE), `main` вҶ’ `origin/main`.
